# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="eb10e-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eb10e-104">応答**secな**要素は、要求に関する状態情報を提供します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="eb10e-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="eb10e-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

<span data-ttu-id="eb10e-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eb10e-1479">注釈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-1479">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eb10e-1480">この要素は必須ではなく、すべての応答に含まれているわけではありません。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-1480">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="eb10e-1481">この要素を記述するスキーマは、Exchange Web サービスをホストする IIS 仮想ディレクトリに置かれています。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eb10e-1481">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
